Firefox DOM Event Dispatch Chain\\n\\n## Event Creation\\nWhen a DOM event is dispatched in Firefox, the process begins in `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp` with the static methods `EventDispatcher::Dispatch()` or `EventDispatcher::DispatchDOMEvent()`. These methods accept a `WidgetEvent*` (the low-level event) and optionally a `dom::Event*` (the DOM-facing event). If a DOM Event is not provided, one is created lazily during dispatch using `EventDispatcher::CreateEvent()`.\\n\\n## Event Target Identification and Chain Building\\nThe event dispatcher constructs an event target chain by iteratively calling `GetEventTargetParent()` on each potential target, starting from the original target and moving up through parent targets. This process is implemented through:\\n\\n- **`EventTargetChainItem::GetEventTargetParent()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:429-444)**: Calls the target's `GetEventTargetParent()` method and caches properties like whether the target wants pre/post-handle events.\\n- **Target-specific implementations** in `dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp`, `dom/base/Document.cpp`, `dom/base/nsWindowRoot.cpp`, and element-specific files like `dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp` that override `GetEventTargetParent()` to set the parent target and handle retargeting (especially important for shadow DOM and anonymous content).\\n\\nThe chain building continues through a while loop in `Dispatch()` (lines 1113-1178) that calls `GetEventTargetParent()` on successive parent targets until no more parents are available or a target indicates it cannot handle the event.\\n\\n## Capture Phase Dispatch\\nOnce the event target chain is built, event dispatch occurs in `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:491-694). The capture phase is implemented as:\\n\\n```cpp\\n// Lines 516-585: Capture phase\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInCapturePhase = true;\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = false;\\nfor (uint32_t i = chainLength - 1; i > firstCanHandleEventTargetIdx; --i) {\\n  EventTargetChainItem& item = chain[i];\\n  // ... event listener invocation ...\\n  item.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThe capture phase iterates BACKWARDS through the event target chain (from the outermost parent down to just before the target), allowing handlers registered in the capture phase to intercept the event before it reaches the target.\\n\\n## Event Listener Invocation\\nListener invocation occurs in `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:339-370), which:\\n\\n1. Calls the target's `WillHandleEvent()` if registered\\n2. Retrieves the target's `EventListenerManager` via `mTarget->GetExistingListenerManager()`\\n3. Calls `EventListenerManager::HandleEvent()` which delegates to `HandleEventInternal()` (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1439-1534)\\n\\n`HandleEventInternal()` performs the actual listener lookup and invocation:\\n- Retrieves listeners for the event type from the listener map\\n- Calls `HandleEventWithListenerArray()` for each listener array\\n- For each listener, invokes `HandleEventSingleListener()` (lines 1233-1295) which:\\n  - Compiles any string-based event handlers\\n  - Calls the listener's `HandleEvent()` method (either WebIDL callback or XPCOM interface)\\n  - Checks for propagation stops and exceptions\\n\\n## Target Phase Dispatch\\nAfter the capture phase completes, the event reaches the target itself (lines 587-611):\\n\\n```cpp\\n// Lines 587-611: Target phase\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInTargetPhase = true;\\nEventTargetChainItem& targetItem = chain[firstCanHandleEventTargetIdx];\\nif (!aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped() && ...) {\\n  targetItem.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);  // Capture listeners\\n}\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInCapturePhase = false;\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = true;\\nif (!aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped() && ...) {\\n  targetItem.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);  // Bubble listeners\\n}\\n```\\n\\nDuring the target phase, both capture-phase and bubble-phase listeners on the target itself are invoked.\\n\\n## Bubble Phase Dispatch\\nFollowing the target phase, if the event bubbles (checked via `aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mBubbles`), the event bubbles up the chain (lines 613-648):\\n\\n```cpp\\n// Lines 613-648: Bubble phase\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = true;\\nfor (uint32_t i = firstCanHandleEventTargetIdx + 1; i < chainLength; ++i) {\\n  EventTargetChainItem& item = chain[i];\\n  if (aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mBubbles || newTarget) {\\n    if (!aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped()) {\\n      item.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);\\n    }\\n  }\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThe bubble phase iterates FORWARDS through the chain (from the target up to the outermost parent), allowing bubble-phase listeners to handle the event.\\n\\n## Default Action Execution\\nDefault action execution is deferred until after all listener phases complete. It occurs in two places:\\n\\n1. **After bubble phase in default event group** (lines 1334-1347): If the event has an activation target (determined during chain building via `mWantsActivationBehavior` in `GetEventTargetParent()`), the dispatcher calls:\\n   - `LegacyCanceledActivationBehavior()` if the event was canceled\\n   - `ActivationBehavior()` if the event was not canceled\\n\\n   These methods delegate to target-specific implementations like `HTMLInputElement::ActivationBehavior()` (dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp) or `HTMLButtonElement::ActivationBehavior()` (dom/html/HTMLButtonElement.cpp).\\n\\n2. **In PostHandleEvent()** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:483-489): Called during the system event group dispatch. Element implementations like `Element::PostHandleEventForLinks()` (dom/base/Element.cpp:4318+) or `HTMLInputElement::PostHandleEvent()` (dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp:3896+) perform default actions such as navigating links or submitting forms.\\n\\n## System Event Group Dispatch\\nAfter the default event group completes, if the event is eligible, the dispatcher repeats the entire capture/target/bubble cycle for the system event group (lines 651-693). This is used for privileged, system-level event listeners that should not be affected by content listeners stopping propagation.\\n\\n## Key Files and Roles\\n\\n- **dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp/h**: Main dispatcher orchestrating the entire flow\\n- **dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp**: Manages registered listeners and invokes them\\n- **dom/events/Event.cpp**: DOM Event object (wraps WidgetEvent)\\n- **dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp**: Pre/post-event state management\\n- **dom/base/Element.cpp, Document.cpp, FragmentOrElement.cpp**: Event target implementations\\n- **dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp, HTMLButtonElement.cpp, etc.**: Element-specific event handling and default actions\\n- **layout/base/PresShell.cpp**: Integration point for layout-triggered events\\n- **widget/nsIWidget.cpp**: Platform widget event dispatch\\n\\nThe event dispatch chain ensures proper isolation of event phases, respects propagation stops, handles event retargeting for shadow DOM, and provides clear separation between listener invocation and default action execution.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2353,"cache_read_input_tokens":95507,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2353},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5d102197-6baf-4427-9d2c-944ae617953e","uuid":"aa7cb9d1-5276-4176-bf78-5411dbbf77f6"}

Firefox DOM Event Dispatch Chain\\n\\n## Event Creation\\nWhen a DOM event is dispatched in Firefox, the process begins in `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp` with the static methods `EventDispatcher::Dispatch()` or `EventDispatcher::DispatchDOMEvent()`. These methods accept a `WidgetEvent*` (the low-level event) and optionally a `dom::Event*` (the DOM-facing event). If a DOM Event is not provided, one is created lazily during dispatch using `EventDispatcher::CreateEvent()`.\\n\\n## Event Target Identification and Chain Building\\nThe event dispatcher constructs an event target chain by iteratively calling `GetEventTargetParent()` on each potential target, starting from the original target and moving up through parent targets. This process is implemented through:\\n\\n- **`EventTargetChainItem::GetEventTargetParent()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:429-444)**: Calls the target's `GetEventTargetParent()` method and caches properties like whether the target wants pre/post-handle events.\\n- **Target-specific implementations** in `dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp`, `dom/base/Document.cpp`, `dom/base/nsWindowRoot.cpp`, and element-specific files like `dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp` that override `GetEventTargetParent()` to set the parent target and handle retargeting (especially important for shadow DOM and anonymous content).\\n\\nThe chain building continues through a while loop in `Dispatch()` (lines 1113-1178) that calls `GetEventTargetParent()` on successive parent targets until no more parents are available or a target indicates it cannot handle the event.\\n\\n## Capture Phase Dispatch\\nOnce the event target chain is built, event dispatch occurs in `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:491-694). The capture phase is implemented as:\\n\\n```cpp\\n// Lines 516-585: Capture phase\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInCapturePhase = true;\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = false;\\nfor (uint32_t i = chainLength - 1; i > firstCanHandleEventTargetIdx; --i) {\\n  EventTargetChainItem& item = chain[i];\\n  // ... event listener invocation ...\\n  item.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThe capture phase iterates BACKWARDS through the event target chain (from the outermost parent down to just before the target), allowing handlers registered in the capture phase to intercept the event before it reaches the target.\\n\\n## Event Listener Invocation\\nListener invocation occurs in `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:339-370), which:\\n\\n1. Calls the target's `WillHandleEvent()` if registered\\n2. Retrieves the target's `EventListenerManager` via `mTarget->GetExistingListenerManager()`\\n3. Calls `EventListenerManager::HandleEvent()` which delegates to `HandleEventInternal()` (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1439-1534)\\n\\n`HandleEventInternal()` performs the actual listener lookup and invocation:\\n- Retrieves listeners for the event type from the listener map\\n- Calls `HandleEventWithListenerArray()` for each listener array\\n- For each listener, invokes `HandleEventSingleListener()` (lines 1233-1295) which:\\n  - Compiles any string-based event handlers\\n  - Calls the listener's `HandleEvent()` method (either WebIDL callback or XPCOM interface)\\n  - Checks for propagation stops and exceptions\\n\\n## Target Phase Dispatch\\nAfter the capture phase completes, the event reaches the target itself (lines 587-611):\\n\\n```cpp\\n// Lines 587-611: Target phase\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInTargetPhase = true;\\nEventTargetChainItem& targetItem = chain[firstCanHandleEventTargetIdx];\\nif (!aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped() && ...) {\\n  targetItem.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);  // Capture listeners\\n}\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInCapturePhase = false;\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = true;\\nif (!aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped() && ...) {\\n  targetItem.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);  // Bubble listeners\\n}\\n```\\n\\nDuring the target phase, both capture-phase and bubble-phase listeners on the target itself are invoked.\\n\\n## Bubble Phase Dispatch\\nFollowing the target phase, if the event bubbles (checked via `aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mBubbles`), the event bubbles up the chain (lines 613-648):\\n\\n```cpp\\n// Lines 613-648: Bubble phase\\naVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mInBubblingPhase = true;\\nfor (uint32_t i = firstCanHandleEventTargetIdx + 1; i < chainLength; ++i) {\\n  EventTargetChainItem& item = chain[i];\\n  if (aVisitor.mEvent->mFlags.mBubbles || newTarget) {\\n    if (!aVisitor.mEvent->PropagationStopped()) {\\n      item.HandleEvent(aVisitor, aCd);\\n    }\\n  }\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThe bubble phase iterates FORWARDS through the chain (from the target up to the outermost parent), allowing bubble-phase listeners to handle the event.\\n\\n## Default Action Execution\\nDefault action execution is deferred until after all listener phases complete. It occurs in two places:\\n\\n1. **After bubble phase in default event group** (lines 1334-1347): If the event has an activation target (determined during chain building via `mWantsActivationBehavior` in `GetEventTargetParent()`), the dispatcher calls:\\n   - `LegacyCanceledActivationBehavior()` if the event was canceled\\n   - `ActivationBehavior()` if the event was not canceled\\n\\n   These methods delegate to target-specific implementations like `HTMLInputElement::ActivationBehavior()` (dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp) or `HTMLButtonElement::ActivationBehavior()` (dom/html/HTMLButtonElement.cpp).\\n\\n2. **In PostHandleEvent()** (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:483-489): Called during the system event group dispatch. Element implementations like `Element::PostHandleEventForLinks()` (dom/base/Element.cpp:4318+) or `HTMLInputElement::PostHandleEvent()` (dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp:3896+) perform default actions such as navigating links or submitting forms.\\n\\n## System Event Group Dispatch\\nAfter the default event group completes, if the event is eligible, the dispatcher repeats the entire capture/target/bubble cycle for the system event group (lines 651-693). This is used for privileged, system-level event listeners that should not be affected by content listeners stopping propagation.\\n\\n## Key Files and Roles\\n\\n- **dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp/h**: Main dispatcher orchestrating the entire flow\\n- **dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp**: Manages registered listeners and invokes them\\n- **dom/events/Event.cpp**: DOM Event object (wraps WidgetEvent)\\n- **dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp**: Pre/post-event state management\\n- **dom/base/Element.cpp, Document.cpp, FragmentOrElement.cpp**: Event target implementations\\n- **dom/html/HTMLInputElement.cpp, HTMLButtonElement.cpp, etc.**: Element-specific event handling and default actions\\n- **layout/base/PresShell.cpp**: Integration point for layout-triggered events\\n- **widget/nsIWidget.cpp**: Platform widget event dispatch\\n\\nThe event dispatch chain ensures proper isolation of event phases, respects propagation stops, handles event retargeting for shadow DOM, and provides clear separation between listener invocation and default action execution.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
